			(

		{
			var anchors=document.getElementsByTagName("a");
			for (var index = 0, count = anchors.length; index < count; ++index)
			{
				var currentElement = anchors[index];
				var elementName = currentElement.innerHTML;
				if (elementName === "Delete")
				{
					anchors[index].addEventListener
					(
						"click",
						function (event) 
						{ 
							if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to delete this record?"))
							{ 
								event.preventDefault(); 
							} 
						},
						false
					);					
				}	
			}	
		}

module.exports = {
	get: function(options, callback)
	{
		http.get(options, function(res){
		  var data = '';

		  res.on('data', function (chunk){
			data += chunk;
		  });

		  res.on('end',function(){
			callback(data);

	}

		<script>
			var LINQLibrary =
			{
				convertToFloat: function (array) {
					var count = array.length;
					for (n = 0; n < count; ++n)
					{
						array[n] = parseFloat(array[n]);
					}
				},

				deepCopy: function( source ) {
					var target = [];
					for (var i = 0, j = source.length; i < j; ++i)
					{
						target[i] = source[i];
					}
					return target;	
				}
			}

			function calculate()
			{
				var dataSet = document.getElementById("request").value;
				var requestArray = dataSet.split(",");
				
				var isNumber = !isNaN(requestArray[0]);
				
				if (isNumber)
				{
					LINQLibrary.convertToFloat(requestArray);
				}
				
				var workingCopy = LINQLibrary.deepCopy(requestArray);

				var count = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Count();
				var distinct = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Distinct().ToArray();
				var first = Enumerable.From(requestArray).First();
				var last = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Last();
				var reverse = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Reverse().ToArray();
				
				if (isNumber)
				{
					var average = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Average();
					var maximum = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Max();
					var minimum = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Min();
					var sum = Enumerable.From(requestArray).Sum();
				}
				else
				{
					var sum = requestArray.join();
				}
				
				var display = "<table border='1'>" +
					"<caption>Statistics</caption>" +
					"<thead><tr><th>Label</th><th>Value</th></tr></thead>" +
					"<tbody>" + 
					((isNumber) ? tabular("Average", average) : "") +
					tabular("Count", count) +
					tabular("Distinct", distinct) +
					tabular("First", first) +
					tabular("Last", last) +
					((isNumber) ? tabular("Maximum", maximum) : "") +
					((isNumber) ? tabular("Minimum", minimum) : "") +
					tabular("Reverse", reverse) +
					tabular(isNumber ? "Sum" : "Concatenate", sum) +
					"</tbody></table>"
					; 
								
				document.getElementById("response").innerHTML = display;	
			}

			function tabular(label, value)
			{
				var formatted = "<tr>" + 
								"<td>" + label + "</td>" + 
								"<td>" + value + "</td>" +
								"</tr>";
				return formatted;
			}
			
			window.addEventListener("load", calculate, false);

			var query = document.getElementById("query");
			query.addEventListener("click", calculate, false);
		</script>

					;

			function tabular(label, value)
			{

								"</tr>";

		public static SqlString UnixEpoch(DateTime dateFrom, DateTime dateTo)
		{
			StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();

			DateTimeOffset dtoFrom = new DateTimeOffset(dateFrom);
			DateTimeOffset dtoTo = new DateTimeOffset(dateTo);
			
			return String.Format
			(
				"{0} ... {1}",
				dtoFrom.ToUnixTimeSeconds(),
				dtoTo.ToUnixTimeSeconds()
			);	
		}

	2178	2017-04-21 12:01:11.800			StringSplitSeparatorHelper.cs	Created. With the split method, consider using character group as separators, for example, rather than having to specify, . ; ?, specify punctuation mark enum type group, and additionally, space character, and/or digits. using System;
using System.Globalization;
using System.Text;

namespace InformationInTransit.ProcessLogic
{
    /*
		2017-04-21	StringSplitSeparatorHelper.cs
		2017-04-21	https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.globalization.unicodecategory(v=vs.110).aspx
		2017-04-21	http://www.alanzucconi.com/2015/07/26/enum-flags-and-bitwise-operators/
		2017-04-21	https://www.dotnetperls.com/tochararray
		2017-04-21	stackoverflow.com/questions/1324009/net-c-sharp-convert-char-to-string
	*/
	public static partial class StringSplitSeparatorHelper
    {
        public static void Main()
        {
			char[] splitCharacters;
			splitCharacters = Combine
			(
				UnicodeCategoryType.ClosePunctuation 
				| UnicodeCategoryType.DashPunctuation
				| UnicodeCategoryType.DecimalDigitNumber
			);
			//splitCharacters = Combine(UnicodeCategoryType.None);
			System.Console.WriteLine(splitCharacters.Length);
			System.Console.WriteLine(new string(splitCharacters));
        }

		public static char[] Combine(UnicodeCategoryType split)
		{
			StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
			if (HasFlag(split, UnicodeCategoryType.ClosePunctuation))
			{
				sb.Append("(){}[]");
			}
			if (HasFlag(split, UnicodeCategoryType.Control))
			{
				sb.Append((char) 0x007F);
				for (int code = 0x0000; code <= 0x001F; ++code)
				{
					
					sb.Append((char)code);
				}
				for (int code = 0x0080; code <= 0x009F; ++code)
				{
					
					sb.Append((char)code);
				}
			}
			if (HasFlag(split, UnicodeCategoryType.DashPunctuation))	
			{
				sb.Append('-');
			}
			if (HasFlag(split, UnicodeCategoryType.DecimalDigitNumber))		
			{
				sb.Append("0123456789");
			}
			return (sb.ToString().ToCharArray());
		}

		// Works with "None" as well
		public static bool HasFlag(UnicodeCategoryType a, UnicodeCategoryType b)
		{
			return (a & b) == b;
		}		
		
		[Flags] 
		public enum UnicodeCategoryType
		{
			// Decimal    				// Binary
			None = 0,					// 000000
			ClosePunctuation = 1,    	// 000001
			Control = 2,				// 000010
			DashPunctuation = 4, 		// 001000
			DecimalDigitNumber = 8
		}		
    }
}

	2206	2017-06-21 19:07:54.357			Placeth.html	Created. 			var isPostBack = false;

			function inputChange(event)
			{
				var columnValue = event.target.value;
				var column = event.target.parentElement;
				var row = column.parentElement;
				var rowIndex = row.rowIndex - 1;
				row.cells[2].innerHTML = 
					(columnValue.trim().toUpperCase() === questionsAndAnswers[rowIndex][1].trim().toUpperCase()) ?
					"Correct" : "Wrong";
			}
			
			function pageLoad()
			{
				if (isPostBack === false)
				{
					var rowCount = questionsAndAnswers.length;
					var	tableContent = 	"<table><thead><caption>Place</caption>" +
										"<tr><th>Question</th><th>Answer</th><th>Result</th></tr>" +
										"</thead><tbody>";
					var	qAndA = document.getElementById("qAndA");
					
					for ( var rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex )
					{
						tableContent += "<tr><td>" + questionsAndAnswers[rowIndex][0] + "</td>" +
							"<td>" + "<input type='text'>" + "</td><td/>" + "</tr>"	
					}
					tableContent += "</tbody></table>";
					qAndA.innerHTML = tableContent;
					
					var inputs = qAndA.getElementsByTagName("input");
					var input;
					for ( var rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex )
					{
						input = inputs[rowIndex];
						input.addEventListener("change", inputChange, false);
					}
				}
				isPostBack = true;
			}
			
			window.addEventListener("load", pageLoad, false);
			
			var questionsAndAnswers = [
				["Ladder", "Bethel"],
				["Place of a skull", "Golgotha"]
			];

<html>
<head>
<!--
	2018-01-01	https://www.w3schools.com/asp/asp_ajax.asp
-->
<script>
function showCustomer(str)
{
	if (str=="")
	{
	  document.getElementById("txtHint").innerHTML="";
	  return;
	}
	if (window.XMLHttpRequest)
	{
		// code for IE7+, Firefox, Chrome, Opera, Safari
		xmlhttp=new XMLHttpRequest();
	}
	else
	{
		// code for IE6, IE5
		xmlhttp=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
	}
	xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function()
	{
		if (this.readyState==4 && this.status==200)
		{
			document.getElementById("txtHint").innerHTML=this.responseText;
		}
		if (this.readyState==4 && this.status==500)
		{
			document.getElementById("txtHint").innerHTML=this.responseText;
		}
	}
	xmlhttp.open("GET","MicrosoftSQLServerDatabaseGetCustomer.asp?q="+str,true);
	xmlhttp.send();
}
</script>
</head
<body>

<form>
<select name="customers" onchange="showCustomer(this.value)">
<option value="">Select a customer:</option>
<option value="ALFKI">Alfreds Futterkiste</option>
<option value="NORTS ">North/South</option>
<option value="WOLZA">Wolski Zajazd</option>
</select>
</form>

</body>
</html>

			{

					//if (connection.hasOwnProperty(key)) {

						{

			}

	3536	2019-01-12 23:18:13.950			Ping.asmx	Created.	public class PingWebService : System.Web.Services.WebService
{
	[WebMethod]
	[ScriptMethod(ResponseFormat = ResponseFormat.Json)]
	public String Query
	(
		string hostNameOrAddress
	)	
    {
		PingReply reply = PingHelper.Query(hostNameOrAddress);
		string json = ""; //JsonConvert.SerializeObject(reply, Formatting.Indented);
		
		json = String.Format
		(
			JsonFormat,
			reply.Address.ToString(),
			reply.RoundtripTime,
			reply.Options.Ttl,
			reply.Buffer.Length,
			reply.Options.DontFragment
		);	
		
		return json;
	}

		function filterData(bookID, bookTitle)
		{
			if (bookID == "All"){
			let chapters = jsonData.filter(data => data.BookTitle==bookTitle)
			.reduce((accumulator, currentValue) => {
			  return accumulator + currentValue.Chapters;
			}, 0)
			return [{'BookID': 'All', 'BookTitle': bookTitle, 'Chapters': chapters}];
			}
			if (bookTitle == "All"){

			.reduce((accumulator, currentValue) => {
				console.log(accumulator);
				return accumulator + currentValue.Chapters;
			}, 0)
			return [{'BookID': bookID, 'BookTitle': 'All', 'Chapters': chapters}];
			}
			let subset = jsonData.filter(data => data.BookID==bookID)
			.filter(data => data.BookTitle== bookTitle);

	(

	3555	2019-02-04 19:01:52.283			IsNecessaryTheSame.html	Created.				function querySubmit()
			{
				var word = document.getElementById("word").value.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '');
				var alphabetSequenceID = parseInt(document.getElementById("alphabetSequenceID").value);
				var letter = String.fromCharCode(96 + alphabetSequenceID);
		
				var occurrences = (word.split(letter).length - 1)
				var combination = letter.repeat(occurrences);
				
				//console.log(letter, occurrences, combination);
				
				word = word.replace(new RegExp(letter, "g"), "");
				
				var index = lettersIndex = 0;
				do
				{
					if (index >= word.length - 1)
					{
						break;
					}	
					lettersIndex += word.charCodeAt(index) - 96;
					//console.log(index, lettersIndex, word, combination);
					if (lettersIndex == alphabetSequenceID)
					{
						combination += word.substring(0, index + 1);
						word = word.substring(1);
						index = lettersIndex = 0;
						continue
					}
					else if (lettersIndex > alphabetSequenceID)
					{
						word = word.substring(1);
						index = lettersIndex = 0;
						continue
					}
					++index;
				} while (word);
				
				document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = combination;
			}

			document.getElementById("submitQuery").addEventListener("click", querySubmit, false);

function toPDF(){       
        var pdf = new jsPDF();

    // source can be HTML-formatted string, or a reference
    // to an actual DOM element from which the text will be scraped.
    //source = $('#frame')[0]
	source = getFrameContents();
	console.log(source);
    // we support special element handlers. Register them with jQuery-style 
    // ID selector for either ID or node name. ("#iAmID", "div", "span" etc.)
    // There is no support for any other type of selectors 
    // (class, of compound) at this time.
    specialElementHandlers = {
        // element with id of "bypass" - jQuery style selector
        'div': function(element, renderer){
            // true = "handled elsewhere, bypass text extraction"
            return true
        }
    }

    // all coords and widths are in jsPDF instance's declared units
    // 'inches' in this case
    pdf.fromHTML(
        source // HTML string or DOM elem ref.
        , 0.5 // x coord
        , 0.5 // y coord
        , {
            'width':7.5 // max width of content on PDF
             ,'elementHandlers': specialElementHandlers
        }
    )

    pdf.save('Test.pdf');
}

function getFrameContents() {
    var iFrame = document.getElementById('targetIframe');
    var iFrameBody;
    if (iFrame.contentDocument) { // FF
        iFrameBody = iFrame.contentDocument.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
    } else if (iFrame.contentWindow) { // IE
        iFrameBody = iFrame.contentWindow.document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
    }
    return iFrameBody.innerHTML
}

			{
				var	dataRow = "";
				var	dataTable = "";
				
				var	bibleWord;
				var words = "";
				var	link;
				var	literal = [];
				
				for (var table in dataSet) 
				{
					dataTable = dataSet[table];
					for (var rowIndex = 0, rowCount = dataTable.length; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex)
					{
						dataRow = dataTable[rowIndex];

								'bibleWord=' + bibleWord;

					}

				var rows = parseInt(document.getElementById("rows").value);
				var columns = parseInt(document.getElementById("columns").value);
				
				var twoDimensionArray = new Array(rows);

				for (var i = 0; i < twoDimensionArray.length; i++)
				{
					twoDimensionArray[i] = new Array(columns);
				}

				for (var y = 0; y < rows; y++)
				{
					for (var x = 0; x < columns; x++)
					{
						twoDimensionArray[y][x] = null;
					}	
				}
				
				var	direction;
				
				var	directionNorth = false;
				var	directionSouth = false;
				
				var	directionWest = false;
				var	directionEast = false;

				var	lengthOfWord;
				
				var	startY, startX;
				
				var notAvailable;
				
				var currentY, currentX;
				
				var wordIndex = 0;
				var wordCount = literal.length;
				
				while ( true )
				{
					bibleWord = literal[wordIndex];
					lengthOfWord = bibleWord.length;

					direction = getRandomIntInclusive(0, 7);
					
					directionNorth = false;
					directionSouth = false;
				
					directionWest = false;
					directionEast = false;
					
					startX = -1;
					startY = -1;

					switch(directions[direction])
					{
						case 'North West':
							directionNorth = true;
							directionWest = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (rows - lengthOfWord + 1));
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive((columns - lengthOfWord + 1), columns - 1);
							break;
						case 'North':
							directionNorth = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (rows - lengthOfWord + 1));
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive(0, columns - 1);
							break;
						case 'North East':
							directionNorth = true;
							directionEast = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (rows - lengthOfWord + 1));
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (columns - lengthOfWord));
							break;
						case 'West':
							directionWest = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(0, rows - 1);
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive((columns - lengthOfWord + 1), columns - 1);
							break;
						case 'East':
							directionEast = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(0, rows -  1);
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (columns - lengthOfWord - 1));
							break;
						case 'South West':
							directionSouth = true;
							directionWest = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive((rows - lengthOfWord) + 1, length);
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive((columns - lengthOfWord + 1), columns - 1);
							break;
						case 'South':
							directionSouth = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive((rows - lengthOfWord) + 1, length);
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive(0, columns - 1);
							break;
						case 'South East':
							directionSouth = true;
							directionEast = true;
							startY = getRandomIntInclusive(rows - 1, (rows - lengthOfWord) + 1);
							startX = getRandomIntInclusive(0, (columns - lengthOfWord - 1));
							break;
					}

					currentY = startY;
					currentX = startX;
					
					for (var position = 0; position < lengthOfWord; ++position)
					{

							twoDimensionArray[currentY][currentX] &&
							literal[wordIndex][position] !=
								twoDimensionArray[currentY][currentX]
						)

							notAvailable = true;
							break;
						}

						{
							++currentY;
						}

						if (directionSouth)
						{
							--currentY;
						}
						
						if (directionWest)
						{
							--currentX;
						}

						if (directionEast)
						{
							++currentX;
						}
					}

					}

					currentX = startX;

							literal[wordIndex][position];
						
						if (directionNorth)
						{
							++currentY;
						}

						if (directionSouth)
						{
							--currentY;
						}
						
						if (directionWest)
						{
							--currentX;
						}

						if (directionEast)
						{
							++currentX;
						}
					}
					
					++wordIndex;
					if (wordIndex >= wordCount)
					{
						break;
					}
				}

					for (var x = 0; x < columns; ++x)

						{

					}

					for (var x = 0; x < columns; ++x)

					crossWordPuzzleTable += "</tr>";
				}

			}

			function querySubmit()
			{
				var event = document.getElementById("event").value;
				var place = document.getElementById("place").value;
				
				var regularExpressionEvent = new RegExp(event, "gi");
				var regularExpressionPlace = new RegExp(place, "gi");

				var queryResult = Enumerable.From(prophecySet)
					.Where
					(
						function(x) 
						{ 
							return x.event.match(regularExpressionEvent) &&	x.place.match(regularExpressionPlace); 	
						}
					)
					.OrderBy(function (x) { return x.event; })
					.Select(function (x) { return x; })
					.ToArray();		
	
				var resultSet = "<table>";
				var currentRecord;
				
				for(var index = 0, length = queryResult.length; index < length; ++index)
				{
					currentRecord = queryResult[index];
					resultSet += "<tr><td><table>";
					for (var property in currentRecord) {
						if (currentRecord.hasOwnProperty(property)) {
							resultSet += `<tr><td>${property}</td><td>${currentRecord[property]}</td></tr>`;
						}
					}
					resultSet += "</table></td></tr>";
				}
	
				resultSet += "</table>";
				
				document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = resultSet;
			}

                  ( 
                      REPLACE(@Command, N'<<DatabaseName>>', QUOTENAME(SD.Name)) 
                      , N'<<LoginName>>' 
                      ,
                      QUOTENAME
                      (
                          COALESCE
                          (
                               SL.name 
                              ,(SELECT TOP 1 name FROM sys.server_principals WHERE type_desc = 'SQL_LOGIN' AND is_disabled = 'false' ORDER BY principal_id ASC )
                          )
                      )
                  ) 
FROM sys.databases AS SD
LEFT JOIN sys.server_principals  AS SL 
    ON SL.SID = SD.owner_sid

//namespace InformationInTransit.ProcessCode
//{
	public partial class ReadFileHelper
	{
		public static void Main(string[] argv)
		{
			ReadFile(argv[0]);
		}
		
		public static void ReadFile(String filename)
		{
			StreamReader	streamReader = new StreamReader(filename);
			String			line;
			SqlPipe			sqlPipe = SqlContext.Pipe;
			
			do
			{
				line = streamReader.ReadLine();
				if (line == null)
				{
					break;
				}
				sqlPipe.Send(line);
			} 
			while (true);
			streamReader.Close();
		}	
	}	
//}

	3579	2019-04-16 14:15:05.147			AlphabetSequence.go	Created.	/*
	2019-04-16	Created.
*/	
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "os"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	length := len(os.Args)
	for i := 1; i < length; i++ {
		fmt.Println(i, os.Args[i], alphabetSequence(os.Args[i]))
	}
}

func alphabetSequence(word string) int{
	word = strings.ToUpper(word)
	var sum int
	sum = 0
	for i, c := range word {
		ascii := int(c)
		i = i
		if (ascii >= 65 && ascii <= 90) {
			sum += ascii - 64;
		}
	}
	return sum
}

	public const string SelectStatement = 
		@"
SELECT 
  SOUNDEX(BibleWord) AS SoundexCode,
  STUFF((
    SELECT ', ' + BibleWord
    FROM Bible..Exact
    WHERE (SOUNDEX(BibleWord) = SOUNDEX(Results.BibleWord))
	AND BibleWord LIKE '%{0}%' AND SOUNDEX(BibleWord) LIKE '%{1}%'
    FOR XML PATH(''),TYPE).value('(./text())[1]','VARCHAR(MAX)')
  ,1,2,'') AS Words
FROM Bible..Exact AS Results
WHERE BibleWord LIKE '%{0}%' AND SOUNDEX(BibleWord) LIKE '%{1}%'
GROUP BY SOUNDEX(BibleWord)
ORDER BY SOUNDEX(BibleWord)
		";
}

[ScriptService]
public class July1951NineteenFiftyOne : System.Web.Services.WebService
{
	[WebMethod]
	[ScriptMethod(ResponseFormat = ResponseFormat.Json)]
	public String Query
	(
		int		bookIDMinimum,
		int		bookIDMaximum,
		string	bookTitle,
		string	sortBy,
		string	sortDirection
	)
    {
		List<BibleBook> dataSet = 
			(
				from BibleBook bibleBook in BibleBook.BibleBooks
				where 
					bibleBook.Id >= bookIDMinimum && 
					bibleBook.Id <= bookIDMaximum &&
					bibleBook.Title.IndexOf(bookTitle, StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase) > -1
				select bibleBook
			).ToList();
			
		dataSet = dataSet.OrderBy(sortBy + " " + sortDirection).ToList();	
			
		string json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(dataSet, Formatting.Indented);
		return json;
	}

	3584	2019-04-23 11:36:21.803			URIWordStatistics.py	Created.	def uriWordStats(uri):
    print(uri)
    f = urlopen(uri)
    fileContent = f.read().decode('utf-8').lower()
    print(fileContent)
    words = re.findall(r"\w+|[^\w\s]", fileContent, re.UNICODE)
    wordStat = dict()
    for word in words:
        occurrence = word in wordStat
        if (occurrence == False):
            wordStat[word] = 1
        else:    
            wordStat[word] += 1
    keys = wordStat.keys()
    for keyCurrent in keys:
        print(keyCurrent, wordStat[keyCurrent])

	3585	2019-04-23 15:59:41.143			URIWordStatistics.html	Created.				var isPostBack = false;
			var uri = "http://www.w3.org/TR/PNG/iso_8859-1.txt";

			function dictionaryKeyValue(words)
			{
				var myMap = new Map();
				
				//myMap.set(NaN, 'not a number');
				var currentWord;
				var wordFound;
				for ( var index = 0, length = words.length; index < length; ++index)
				{
					currentWord = words[index].trim();
					wordFound = myMap.has(currentWord);
					if (!wordFound)
					{
						myMap.set(currentWord, 1);
					}
					else
					{
						myMap.set(currentWord, myMap.get(currentWord) + 1);
					}
				}
				
				return myMap;
			}

					querySubmit();

			{

				.then((res) => {
					  return res.text();
				})
				.then((data) => {
					document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = data;
					var regex = /[ ,;.(){}^/'"]+/gi;
					//var regex = /\b/;
					var words = data.toLowerCase().split(regex);
					var myMap = dictionaryKeyValue(words);
					var htmlTable = "<table id='tableURI'><thead><tr><th>Key</th><th>Value</th></tr></thead><tbody>";
					for (var [key, value] of myMap) {
						htmlTable += "<tr><td>" + key + "</td><td>" + value + "</td></tr>";
					}
					htmlTable += "</tbody></table>";
					document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = htmlTable;
					tsorter.create("tableURI");
				});
			}

	3586	2019-04-24 12:36:17.753			GoalKicker_-_DateTimeHelper.py	Created.	"""
2019-04-23 Created.	goalkicker.com/PythonBook
2019-04-23 https://stackoverflow.com/questions/466345/converting-string-into-datetime
2019-04-23 http://book.pythontips.com/en/latest/ternary_operators.html

def dateDiff(datedFrom, datedUntil):
    #datedFrom = datetime.strptime(datedFrom, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S%z")
    #datedUntil = datetime.strptime(datedUntil, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S%z")
    datedFrom = datetime.fromisoformat(datedFrom)
    datedUntil = datetime.fromisoformat(datedUntil)
    delta = datedUntil-datedFrom
    print(delta.days, " days")
    biblicalYear = int(delta.days / 360)
    biblicalMonth = int((delta.days - biblicalYear * 360) / 30)
    biblicalDay = (delta.days - biblicalYear * 360) % 30
    biblicalDuration = ""
    if (biblicalYear > 0):
        biblicalDuration += str(biblicalYear) + " Biblical Year" + ("s" if (biblicalYear > 1) else "")
    if (biblicalMonth > 0):
        biblicalDuration += ("" if (biblicalDuration == "") else ", ") + str(biblicalMonth) + " Biblical Month" + ("s" if (biblicalMonth > 1) else "")
    if (biblicalDay > 0):
        biblicalDuration += ("" if (biblicalDuration == "") else ", ") + str(biblicalDay) + " Day"  + ("s" if (biblicalDay > 1) else "")
    print(biblicalDuration)    
    return

def get_n_days_after_date(date_format="%d %B %Y", add_days=120):
    date_n_days_after = datetime.datetime.now() + timedelta(days=add_days)
    return date_n_days_after.strftime(date_format)

	3587	2019-04-24 15:20:32.750			BibleBook.py	Created.	#2019-03-05	pip install pyodbc
from flask import Flask
import pyodbc
app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/")
def hello():
    return "Hello World!"

@app.route('/bibleBooks')
def bibleBooks():
    queryStatement = "SELECT DISTINCT BookID, BookTitle FROM Scripture ORDER BY BookID"
    return sqlSelect(queryStatement)

@app.route('/bibleBook/<bookTitle>')
def bibleBook(bookTitle):
    queryStatement = "SELECT DISTINCT BookID, BookTitle FROM Scripture WHERE BookTitle LIKE '%" + bookTitle + "%' ORDER BY BookID"
    return sqlSelect(queryStatement)

def sqlSelect(selectQuery):
    cnxn = pyodbc.connect("Driver={SQL Server Native Client 11.0};"
                          "Server=(local);"
                          "Database=Bible;"
                          "Trusted_Connection=yes;")
    cursor = cnxn.cursor()
    cursor.execute(selectQuery)
    result_set = cursor.fetchall()
    
    infoSet = "<table border='1'>"

    for row in result_set:
        infoSet += "<tr><td>" + str(row[0]) + "</td><td>" + row[1] + "</td></tr>"

    infoSet += "</table>"
    
    return infoSet

	3588	2019-04-26 22:38:16.727	Genesis 2:7, Genesis 3:14, Genesis 3:17-19, Genesis 4:10-12		NoticingTheSame.html	Created.				var isPostBack = false;
			
			function buildHyperlink(address, parameter) 
			{
				if (!parameter) { return ""; }
				var prefix = "";
				if (address.toLowerCase().indexOf("http") === -1)
				{
					prefix = "/WordEngineering/WordUnion/"; 
				}
				var uri = encodeURI(prefix + address + ".html?" + address + "=" + parameter);
				var hyperlink = "<a href=" + uri + ">" + parameter + "</a>";
				return hyperlink;
			}
			
			function pageLoad()
			{
				if (isPostBack === false)
				{
					populate();
					querySubmit();
					isPostBack = true;
				}
			}
			
			function populate()
			{
				var dataDefinitionLanguage =
					`
						CREATE TABLE noticingTheSame 
						( 
							Event string,
							Actor string,
							ScriptureReference string,
							Place string
						)
					`;
				alasql(dataDefinitionLanguage);

				var dataManipulationLanguage =
					`
						INSERT INTO noticingTheSame VALUES
						(
							'Creation',
							'God',
							'Genesis 1',
							'Heaven, Earth'
						),
						(
							'The Fall of Man',

							null
						)						
					`;
				alasql(dataManipulationLanguage);
			}
			
			function querySubmit()
			{
				var question = document.getElementById("question").value;
				var res = alasql
				(
					`SELECT * FROM noticingTheSame WHERE 
						Event LIKE '%${question}%'
						OR Actor LIKE '%${question}%'
						OR ScriptureReference LIKE '%${question}%'
						OR Place LIKE '%${question}%'
					`
				);    
				document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = render(res, "table0");
				tsorter.create("table0");
			}
	
			function render(data, dataID)
			{
				var dataRow = null;
				var dataTable = null;
				var cellContent = null;
				var cellName = null;
				var cells = "<th>#</th>";
				var info = "";
				var detailKeys = null;
				var detailRow = null;
				var value = null;
				
				info += "<table id='" + dataID + "'>";

				var occurrences = data.length;
				var caption = "<caption>Occurrences: " + occurrences + "</caption>";
				
				info += caption;
				
				dataTable = data;
				
				if (dataTable.length < 1)
				{
					return "";
				}	

				dataRow = dataTable[0];
				
				dataKeys = Object.keys(dataRow);
				for (var dataIndex = 0, dataCount = dataKeys.length; dataIndex < dataCount; ++dataIndex)
				{
					cells += "<th>" + dataKeys[dataIndex] + "</th>";
				}
				
				info += "<thead><tr>" + cells + "</tr></thead>";
				
				for (var rowIndex = 0, rowCount = dataTable.length; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex)
				{
					dataRow = dataTable[rowIndex];
					cells = "<td>" + (rowIndex + 1) + "</td>"
			
					for (var dataIndex = 0, dataCount = dataKeys.length; dataIndex < dataCount; ++dataIndex)
					{
						cellName = dataKeys[dataIndex];
						cellContent = dataRow[cellName];
						
						if (!cellContent)
						{
							cellContent = "";
						}
						
						else if (cellName.includes("ScriptureReference"))
						{
							cellContent = buildHyperlink("scriptureReference", cellContent);
						}		
						else if (cellName.includes("Place"))
						{
							cellContent = buildHyperlink("bibleWord", cellContent);
						}		
						cells += "<td>" + cellContent + "</td>";
					}

					info += "<tr>" + cells + "</tr>";
				}
					
				info += "</table>"
			
				return info;
			}

			function buildHyperlink(address, parameter) 
			{
				if (!parameter) { return ""; }
				var prefix = "";
				if (address.toLowerCase().indexOf("http") === -1)
				{
					prefix = "/WordEngineering/WordUnion/"; 
				}
				var uri = encodeURI(prefix + address + ".html?" + address + "=" + parameter);
				var hyperlink = "<a href=" + uri + ">" + parameter + "</a>";
				return hyperlink;
			}
			
			function pageLoad()
			{
				if (isPostBack === false)
				{
					populate();
					querySubmit();
					isPostBack = true;
				}
			}

			function querySubmit()
			{
				var question = document.getElementById("question").value;
				var res = alasql
				(
					`SELECT * FROM ThatIsNotWhereHisVoiceIsAt WHERE 
						Feature LIKE '%${question}%'
						OR ScriptureReference LIKE '%${question}%'
					`
				);    
				document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = render(res, "table0");
				tsorter.create("table0");
			}
	
			function render(data, dataID)
			{
				var dataRow = null;
				var dataTable = null;
				var cellContent = null;
				var cellName = null;
				var cells = "<th>#</th>";
				var info = "";
				var detailKeys = null;
				var detailRow = null;
				var value = null;
				
				info += "<table id='" + dataID + "'>";

				var occurrences = data.length;
				var caption = "<caption>Occurrences: " + occurrences + "</caption>";
				
				info += caption;
				
				dataTable = data;
				
				if (dataTable.length < 1)
				{
					return "";
				}	

				dataRow = dataTable[0];
				
				dataKeys = Object.keys(dataRow);
				for (var dataIndex = 0, dataCount = dataKeys.length; dataIndex < dataCount; ++dataIndex)
				{
					cells += "<th>" + dataKeys[dataIndex] + "</th>";
				}
				
				info += "<thead><tr>" + cells + "</tr></thead>";
				
				for (var rowIndex = 0, rowCount = dataTable.length; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex)
				{
					dataRow = dataTable[rowIndex];
					cells = "<td>" + (rowIndex + 1) + "</td>"
			
					for (var dataIndex = 0, dataCount = dataKeys.length; dataIndex < dataCount; ++dataIndex)
					{
						cellName = dataKeys[dataIndex];
						cellContent = dataRow[cellName];
						
						if (!cellContent)
						{
							cellContent = "";
						}
						
						else if (cellName.includes("ScriptureReference"))
						{
							cellContent = buildHyperlink("scriptureReference", cellContent);
						}		
						else if (cellName.includes("Feature"))
						{
							cellContent = buildHyperlink("bibleWord", cellContent);
						}		
						cells += "<td>" + cellContent + "</td>";
					}

					info += "<tr>" + cells + "</tr>";
				}
					
				info += "</table>"
			
				return info;
			}

class ArgumentType():
    # Initializer / Instance Attributes
    def __init__(self, passed):
        self.passed = passed

    # instance method
    def toString(self):
        return "Argument: {} Type: {}".format(self.passed, type(self.passed))

def parseEntry(entry):
    if entry.isdigit():
        entry = int(entry)
    elif entry.replace('.','',1).isdigit() and entry.count('.') < 2:
        entry = float(entry)
    return entry
    
if __name__ == '__main__':
    import sys
    # Instantiate the ArgumentType object
    # arguments = sys.argv[1].split(',')
    for i in range(1, len(sys.argv)):
        currentArgument = ArgumentType(parseEntry(sys.argv[i]))
        print(currentArgument.toString())

	2019-05-31	Created.

import java.io.*;
public class AlphabetSequence {
	public static void main(String args[]) {
		for	( String arg : args ) {
			String upperCase = arg.toUpperCase();
			long alphabetSequenceIndex = 0;
			for(char character : upperCase.toCharArray()) {
				if (character >= 'A' && character <= 'Z')
				{
					alphabetSequenceIndex += (int) character - 64;
				}			
			}
			System.out.format("Word: %s AlphabetSequence: %d\n", arg, alphabetSequenceIndex);
		}			
	}   
}

			function tableRowsIterate()
			{
				dataTable = document.getElementById("dataTable");
				dataRow = document.getElementById("dataRow");
				var tableStyle = "";
				for
				(
					var rowIndex = 0, rowsCount = dataTable.rows.length;
					rowIndex < rowsCount;
					rowIndex++
				)
				{		
					var element = dataTable.rows[rowIndex];
					var style = getComputedStyle(element)
					var rowStyle = 	`
										TableRowIndex:${rowIndex}
										| Style.backgroundColor: ${style.backgroundColor} 
										| Style.color: ${style.color}
										<br/>
									`;	
					tableStyle += rowStyle;				
				}
				document.getElementById("resultSet").innerHTML = tableStyle;
			}

from flask import Flask
app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/")
def hello():
    return "Hello World!"

@app.route('/bibleBooks')
def bibleBooks():
    return query()

@app.route('/bibleBook/<bookTitle>')
def bibleBook(bookTitle):
    return query(bookTitle)

def readFile():
	infile = open("BibleBook.txt", "r")
	for line in infile.readlines():
		columns = line.split(",")
		bookID = columns[0]
		bookTitle = columns[1]
		chapters = columns[2]
		bibleBooks[bookTitle] = chapters
		
def query(bookTitle = ""):
    infoSet = "<table border='1'>"
    bookID = 0
    for the_key, the_value in bibleBooks.items():
        bookID += 1
        if (bookTitle == "" or the_key.find(bookTitle) > -1):
            infoSet += "<tr><td>" + str(bookID) + "</td><td>" + the_key + "</td><td>" + the_value + "</td></tr>"
    infoSet += "</table>"
    return infoSet

bibleBooks = {}
readFile()

	3690	2020-03-21 16:38:09.370	1 Samuel 1:1		ARecordToBeSomeoneElse.html	Created.	CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_BibleBooksAuthor]
AS
--2020-03-21	https://stackoverflow.com/questions/12668528/sql-server-group-by-clause-to-get-comma-separated-values
SELECT Author, BibleBooks = 
    STUFF((SELECT ', ' + bookTitle
           FROM Bible..BibleBook BibleBookSecond
           WHERE BibleBookFirst.Author = BibleBookSecond.Author
          FOR XML PATH('')), 1, 2, '')
FROM Bible..BibleBook AS BibleBookFirst
GROUP BY Author
ORDER BY Author

	3694	2020-04-01 16:46:26.030			DaneHillard_-_Ithaka.py	Created.	"""

from apiron import JsonEndpoint, Service

class GitHub(Service):
    domain = 'https://api.github.com'
    user = JsonEndpoint(path='/users/{username}')
    repo = JsonEndpoint(path='/repos/{org}/{repo}')
	
response = GitHub.user(username='defunkt')
print(response)
# {"name": "Chris Wanstrath", ...}
print("name: ", response["name"])

response = GitHub.repo(org='github', repo='hub')
print(response)
# {"description": "hub helps you win at git.", ...}
print("description: ", response["description"])

#include <algorithm>
#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

using namespace std;

void f(vector<string>& v)
{
    string val;
    cin >> val;
    std::vector<string>::iterator p = find(begin(v), end(v), val);
	cout<< *p << endl;
}

int main(int argc, char *argv[]) 
{
	std::vector<std::string> v = { "Genesis", "Exodus", "Leviticus", "Numbers", "Deuteronomy" };
	f(v);
}
